{\em value} & output read value \\
\hline
{\em dot} & decimal point character \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} object storing a past-\/the-\/end pointer (on success) and an error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Analyzes the character sequence \mbox{[}first,last) for a floating point pattern. If no characters match the pattern, value is set to 0, otherwise the characters matching the pattern are interpreted as a text representation of an arithmetic value, which is stored in value.

Nan and infinit values (upper or lower case) are handled by this function.

This function is simillar to C++17 std\+::from\+\_\+chars with the following differences\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Leading spaces are consumed.
\item If the pattern is a valid floating point text representation too large or too small to be stored in given output value, value will be set to (+-\/)inf or (+-\/)0, and the full pattern will be consumed. Therefore, std\+::errc\+::result\+\_\+out\+\_\+of\+\_\+range is never returned.
\item Leading \textquotesingle{}+\textquotesingle{} sign is considered valid.
\item This function is not an exact parser. In some cases it relies on unprecise floating point arithmetic wich might produce different roundings than strtod() function. Note that the result is almost always equal to the result of strtod, and potential differences are located in the last digits. Use this function when the speed factor is more important than 100\% perfect exactitude.
\end{DoxyItemize}

On success, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{seq\+::from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ptr points at the first character not matching the pattern, or has the value equal to last if all characters match and ec is value-\/initialized.

If there is no pattern match, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ptr equals first and ec equals std\+::errc\+::invalid\+\_\+argument. value is set to 0. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_aac6fa5dbb2342554b8e0229a2517c05e}\label{namespaceseq_aac6fa5dbb2342554b8e0229a2517c05e}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!from\_chars@{from\_chars}}
\index{from\_chars@{from\_chars}!seq@{seq}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from\_chars()}{from\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class T $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::from\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{T \&}]{value,  }\item[{int}]{base = {\ttfamily 10} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read an integral value from the sequence of characters \mbox{[}first,last). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em first} & first character of the sequence \\
\hline
{\em last} & past-\/the-\/end character \\
\hline
{\em value} & output read value \\
\hline
{\em base} & integer base (default to 10) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} object storing a past-\/the-\/end pointer (on success) and an error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Analyzes the character sequence \mbox{[}first,last) for an integral pattern. If no characters match the pattern, value is set to 0, otherwise the characters matching the pattern are interpreted as a text representation of an arithmetic value, which is stored in value.

This function is similar to std\+::from\+\_\+chars except for the following situations\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}- For hexadecimal numbers, the (potential) '0x' prefix will be automatically detected and handled.
- Leading spaces are consumed.
- Leading '+' sign is valid.
- If the pattern is a valid integral text representation too large to be stored in a value, the full pattern will still be consumed,
the function will return a 'success' from_chars_result, and value will silently overflow.
- Reading a negative text representation in an unsigned variable is NOT valid.
\end{DoxyVerb}


On success, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{seq\+::from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ptr points at the first character not matching the pattern, or has the value equal to last if all characters match and ec is value-\/initialized.

If there is no pattern match, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1from__chars__result}{from\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ptr equals first and ec equals std\+::errc\+::invalid\+\_\+argument. value is set to 0. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a9a68123ed035fdbc90e3a4dbe10c7017}\label{namespaceseq_a9a68123ed035fdbc90e3a4dbe10c7017}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!from\_stream@{from\_stream}}
\index{from\_stream@{from\_stream}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from\_stream()}{from\_stream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Stream $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} Stream\& seq\+::from\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Stream \&}]{str,  }\item[{double \&}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a19a45e1f866d73140819b9ea2280c682}{chars\+\_\+format}}}]{fmt = {\ttfamily chars\+\_\+format\+:\+:general},  }\item[{char}]{dot = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read a floating point value from a \#basic\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & stream object to read from \\
\hline
{\em value} & output read value \\
\hline
{\em dot} & dot character, usually \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{} for \textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{} locale. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
reference to the stream object
\end{DoxyReturn}
Analyzes the stream for a floating point pattern. If no characters match the pattern, value is set to 0, otherwise the characters matching the pattern are interpreted as a text representation of an floating point value, which is stored in value.

Nan and infinit values (upper or lower case) are handled by this function.

If the parsing fails (no floating point pattern was detected), the stream status will be set to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ac3d7eb5b00b5c7e90602aaf0e8bd23e2a255aad079a8bea265f55d1a6e8ef5587}{Bad\+Input\+Format}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ac3d7eb5b00b5c7e90602aaf0e8bd23e2a3f7afd64256598243b4355a79f0e4d7d}{End\+Of\+File}} depending on the situation, and stream get position will be reverted to its original state.

This function is simillar to C++17 std\+::from\+\_\+chars with the following differences\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Leading spaces are consumed.
\item If the pattern is a valid floating point text representation too large or too small to be stored in given output value, value will be set to (+-\/)inf or (+-\/)0, and the full pattern will be consumed. Therefore, std\+::errc\+::result\+\_\+out\+\_\+of\+\_\+range is never returned.
\item Leading \textquotesingle{}+\textquotesingle{} sign is considered valid.
\item This function is not an exact parser. In some cases it relies on unprecise floating point arithmetic wich might produce different roundings than strtod() function. Note that the result is almost always equal to the result of strtod(), and potential differences are located in the last digits. Use this function when the speed factor is more important than 100\% perfect exactitude.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This function is usefull when you need to read a huge amount of floating point values of a std\+::istream object. Internal benchmarks show that using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a8dd14a20a2e7b03cebe3d48e3ae5e2ff}{from\+\_\+stream()}} is around 20 faster (or more) than using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a368335418326de8bb38c9fba7642c027}{std\+::istream\+::operator$>$$>$()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ad1f5c92eee4485b984df28c1ceb0f96a}{seq\+::from\+\_\+chars}} internally uses \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a8dd14a20a2e7b03cebe3d48e3ae5e2ff}{seq\+::from\+\_\+stream}} with a \mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1buffer__input__stream}{seq\+::buffer\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream}} object. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_ac74a811757834955b06125e00c5deaed}\label{namespaceseq_ac74a811757834955b06125e00c5deaed}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!from\_stream@{from\_stream}}
\index{from\_stream@{from\_stream}!seq@{seq}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from\_stream()}{from\_stream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Stream $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} Stream\& seq\+::from\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Stream \&}]{str,  }\item[{std\+::string \&}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read a word from a \#basic\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & stream object \\
\hline
{\em value} & output string object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
reference to the stream object
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read a full word from a stream object. In a text files, words are delimited by white-\/space characters (\textquotesingle{} \textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}t\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}v\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}f\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}r\textquotesingle{}, E\+OF). If no string was read because the get position was after the last stream character, the value string is cleared and stream state is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ac3d7eb5b00b5c7e90602aaf0e8bd23e2a3f7afd64256598243b4355a79f0e4d7d}{End\+Of\+File}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a8dd14a20a2e7b03cebe3d48e3ae5e2ff}\label{namespaceseq_a8dd14a20a2e7b03cebe3d48e3ae5e2ff}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!from\_stream@{from\_stream}}
\index{from\_stream@{from\_stream}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from\_stream()}{from\_stream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [5/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Stream , class T $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} Stream\& seq\+::from\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Stream \&}]{str,  }\item[{T \&}]{value,  }\item[{int}]{base = {\ttfamily 10} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read an integral value from a \mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1basic__input__stream}{seq\+::basic\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream}} object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & stream object to read from \\
\hline
{\em value} & output read value \\
\hline
{\em base} & integer base (default to 10) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
reference to the stream object
\end{DoxyReturn}
Analyzes the stream for an integral pattern. If no characters match the pattern or if the value obtained by parsing the matched characters is not representable in the type of value, value is set to 0, otherwise the characters matching the pattern are interpreted as a text representation of an arithmetic value, which is stored in value.

For hexadecimal numbers, the (potential) \textquotesingle{}0x\textquotesingle{} prefix will be automatically detected and handled. Leading spaces are consumed. If the pattern is a valid integral text representation too large to be stored in a value, the full pattern will still be consumed. Reading a negative text representation in an unsigned variable is not valid.

If the parsing fails (no integral pattern was detected), the stream status will be set to Bad\+Input\+Format or End\+Of\+File depending on the situation.

\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ad1f5c92eee4485b984df28c1ceb0f96a}{seq\+::from\+\_\+chars}} internally uses \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a8dd14a20a2e7b03cebe3d48e3ae5e2ff}{seq\+::from\+\_\+stream}} with a \mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1buffer__input__stream}{seq\+::buffer\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream}} object. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_aff00103371136fa3e5dd96eb74a400bb}\label{namespaceseq_aff00103371136fa3e5dd96eb74a400bb}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!from\_stream@{from\_stream}}
\index{from\_stream@{from\_stream}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from\_stream()}{from\_stream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Stream , size\+\_\+t Ss, class Al $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} Stream\& seq\+::from\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Stream \&}]{str,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1tiny__string}{tiny\+\_\+string}}$<$ Ss, Al $>$ \&}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read a word from a \#basic\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & stream object \\
\hline
{\em value} & output string object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
reference to the stream object
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read a full word from a stream object. In a text files, words are delimited by white-\/space characters (\textquotesingle{} \textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}t\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}v\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}f\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}r\textquotesingle{}, E\+OF). If no string was read because the get position was after the last stream character, the value string is cleared and stream state is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ac3d7eb5b00b5c7e90602aaf0e8bd23e2a3f7afd64256598243b4355a79f0e4d7d}{End\+Of\+File}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_aca5e1bd8af52c82c89100c6146c47e10}\label{namespaceseq_aca5e1bd8af52c82c89100c6146c47e10}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$size\+\_\+t Size, class Al $>$ \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a6eb611395bcf177863d2e3bb53432afc}\label{namespaceseq_a6eb611395bcf177863d2e3bb53432afc}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!operator==@{operator==}}
\index{operator==@{operator==}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator==()}{operator==()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/11]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Key , class T , class Compare , class Al1 , class Al2 , Layout\+Management L1, Layout\+Management L2, bool S1, bool S2, bool U1, bool U2$>$ \\
bool seq\+::operator== (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1flat__map}{flat\+\_\+map}}$<$ Key, T, Compare, Al1, L1, S1, U1 $>$ \&}]{s1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classseq_1_1flat__map}{flat\+\_\+map}}$<$ Key, T, Compare, Al2, L2, S2, U2 $>$ \&}]{s2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Checks if the contents of s1 and s2 are equal, that is, they have the same number of elements and each element in s1 compares equal with the element in s2 at the same position.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Stream $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} Stream\& seq\+::read\+\_\+line\+\_\+from\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Stream \&}]{str,  }\item[{std\+::string \&}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read a line from a \#basic\+\_\+input\+\_\+stream object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & stream object \\
\hline
{\em value} & output string object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
reference to the stream object
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read a full line from a stream object. In a text files, lines are delimited by characters \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}r\textquotesingle{} or E\+OF. If no string was read because the get position was after the last stream character, the value string is cleared and stream state is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_ac3d7eb5b00b5c7e90602aaf0e8bd23e2a3f7afd64256598243b4355a79f0e4d7d}{End\+Of\+File}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a68c61bfb64e7882fc5018cad8cb51fd4}\label{namespaceseq_a68c61bfb64e7882fc5018cad8cb51fd4}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void seq\+::tick (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a295df44c0aa1b1bd24f09fc99530a445}\label{namespaceseq_a295df44c0aa1b1bd24f09fc99530a445}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{bool}]{value,  }\item[{int}]{base = {\ttfamily 10},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format}} \&}]{fmt = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format}}()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [delete]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_ad80e2e70627dd4598cda06a37b7767b6}\label{namespaceseq_ad80e2e70627dd4598cda06a37b7767b6}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{char}]{value,  }\item[{int}]{base = {\ttfamily 10},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format}} \&}]{fmt = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format}}()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Converts value into a character string by successively filling the range \mbox{[}first, last), where \mbox{[}first, last) is required to be a valid range. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em first} & first output character \\
\hline
{\em last} & past-\/the-\/end character \\
\hline
{\em value} & input value to convert to string \\
\hline
{\em base} & integer base (default to 10) \\
\hline
{\em fmt} & optional format \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} object
\end{DoxyReturn}
value is converted to a string of digits in the given base (with no redundant leading zeroes by default). Digits in the range 10..35 (inclusive) are represented as lowercase characters a..z by default. If value is less than zero, the representation starts with a minus sign. The library provides overloads for all signed and unsigned integer types and for the type char as the type of the parameter value. This function produces a similar output as std\+::to\+\_\+chars.

Output formatting can be controlled through a \#integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format object\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Digits in the range 10..35 (inclusive) can be represented as uppercase characters A..Z with \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format_acafd17ef17d30b606b9c7087ec7e8d73}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format\+::upper\+\_\+case}}
\item For base 16, a trailing \textquotesingle{}0x\textquotesingle{} can be added with \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format_adbac65c685a9d5c9021e228cee354eed}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format\+::hex\+\_\+prefix}}
\item A minimum width (in number of digits) can be specified to add leading zeros with \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1integral__chars__format_a7fd219f1f9f4a2d0760313d06a378f3a}{integral\+\_\+chars\+\_\+format\+::integral\+\_\+min\+\_\+width}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

On success, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{seq\+::to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ec equals value-\/initialized std\+::errc and ptr is the one-\/past-\/the-\/end pointer of the characters written. Note that the string is not N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated.

On error, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{seq\+::to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} holding std\+::errc\+::value\+\_\+too\+\_\+large in ec, a copy of the value last in ptr, and leaves the contents of the range\mbox{[}first, last) in unspecified state. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a55bcd11b01a3f09227c80c355d84c28d}\label{namespaceseq_a55bcd11b01a3f09227c80c355d84c28d}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{double}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_aa2ce07ea09c6b1253bd62111853a01fc}\label{namespaceseq_aa2ce07ea09c6b1253bd62111853a01fc}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{double}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a19a45e1f866d73140819b9ea2280c682}{chars\+\_\+format}}}]{fmt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_abe570a1e00892b6ed78277b2939477fd}\label{namespaceseq_abe570a1e00892b6ed78277b2939477fd}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [5/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{double}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a19a45e1f866d73140819b9ea2280c682}{chars\+\_\+format}}}]{fmt,  }\item[{int}]{precision,  }\item[{char}]{dot = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{char}]{exp = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{bool}]{upper = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a00b551a6b9a237e00485171e598b17ed}\label{namespaceseq_a00b551a6b9a237e00485171e598b17ed}} 
\index{seq@{seq}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!seq@{seq}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{float}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Converts value into a character string by successively filling the range \mbox{[}first, last), where \mbox{[}first, last) is required to be a valid range. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em first} & first output character \\
\hline
{\em last} & past-\/the-\/end character \\
\hline
{\em value} & input value to convert to string \\
\hline
{\em fmt} & floating-\/point formatting to use, a bitmask of type \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a19a45e1f866d73140819b9ea2280c682}{seq\+::chars\+\_\+format}} \\
\hline
{\em precision} & maximum digits after the radix point \\
\hline
{\em fmt} & optional format \\
\hline
{\em dot} & optional decimal point sequence, default to \char`\"{}.\char`\"{} \\
\hline
{\em exp} & optional exponential character, default to \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} object
\end{DoxyReturn}
value is converted to a string as if by std\+::printf in the default (\char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{}) locale (with some differences, see below). This function D\+O\+ES N\+OT provide exact formatting of the input unlike printf familly of functions.

The conversion specifier is \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{} (resolving in favor of f in case of a tie), chosen according to the requirement for a shortest representation\+: the string representation consists of the smallest number of characters such that there is at least one digit before the radix point (if present).

The conversion specified for the as-\/if printf is \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{} if fmt is seq\+::chars\+\_\+format\+::fixed, \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{} if fmt is seq\+::chars\+\_\+format\+::scientific, and \textquotesingle{}g\textquotesingle{} if fmt is chars\+\_\+format\+::general (default).

If the precision is specified by the parameter \textquotesingle{}precision\textquotesingle{}, this function will output up-\/to (but to necessarily exactly) \textquotesingle{}precision\textquotesingle{} digits after the radix point. The default precision is 6. This function will always try to output the smallest possible character sequence. If \textquotesingle{}dot\textquotesingle{} is specified, it will replace the \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{} decimal point used by the \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} locale.

If \textquotesingle{}exp\textquotesingle{} is specified, it will replace the \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{} exponent character used by the \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} locale.

NaN and infinit values are handled by this function.

On success, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{seq\+::to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} such that ec equals value-\/initialized std\+::errc and ptr is the one-\/past-\/the-\/end pointer of the characters written. Note that the string is not N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated.

On error, returns a value of type \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{seq\+::to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} holding std\+::errc\+::value\+\_\+too\+\_\+large in ec, a copy of the value last in ptr, and leaves the contents of the range\mbox{[}first, last) in unspecified state.

There are currently a lot of different algorithms to provide fast and exact convertion of floating point values to strings\+: ryu, grisu-\/exact, dragonbox... This function tries to provide a faster and lighter alternative when exact precision is not a requirement (which is my case). Internal benchmarks show that convertiing double values to string using this function is around 2 times faster than with ryu library for scientific or general formatting, and 3 times faster with fixed formatting.

When converting double values, obtained strings are similar to the result of printf in 100\% of the cases when the required precision is below 12. After that, the ratio decreases to 87\% of exactitude for a precision of 17. Converting a very high (or very small) value with the \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{} specifier will usually produce slightly different output, especially in the \char`\"{}garbade\char`\"{} digits.

Use this function when you need very fast formatting of a huge amount of floating point values without exact formatting requirement. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceseq_a9eaa974695ff6a6769addd3a96b41404}\label{namespaceseq_a9eaa974695ff6a6769addd3a96b41404}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__bits_ga68ad5ff4a759a2a341569a42f9ba2e44}{S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+A\+L\+W\+A\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq_1_1to__chars__result}{to\+\_\+chars\+\_\+result}} seq\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{float}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceseq_a19a45e1f866d73140819b9ea2280c682}{chars\+\_\+format}}}]{fmt,  }\item[{int}]{precision,  }\item[{char}]{dot = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{char}]{exp = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{bool}]{upper = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}
